# FEATURE_REGISTRY.md

# My Gujarat Property — Feature Registry

This file is the master feature, module, route, database, provider and QA tracking registry for **My Gujarat Property**.

Claude must update this file after every phase and every implementation change.

No feature, route, module, table, permission, provider dependency or QA item should silently disappear from the project.

---

## 1. Registry Rules

Claude must use this registry as the single tracking source for feature status.

Every feature must have:

* feature ID
* feature/module name
* area
* allowed roles
* expected routes
* expected database objects
* provider dependency
* current status
* QA status
* manual verification status
* security/RLS status
* notes
* last updated phase

Claude must update this file when:

* a feature starts
* a feature is completed
* a feature is partially completed
* a feature is blocked
* a feature needs provider setup
* a feature changes routes
* a feature adds/changes DB tables
* a feature adds/changes RLS policies
* a feature adds/changes storage buckets
* a feature adds/changes permissions
* a feature adds/changes UI states
* a feature fails verification
* a feature passes verification

---

## 2. Allowed Status Values

Use only these status values:

| Status             | Meaning                                                                        |
| ------------------ | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------ |
| `NOT_STARTED`      | Feature has not been implemented yet                                           |
| `IN_PROGRESS`      | Feature is currently being implemented                                         |
| `DONE`             | Feature implementation is completed                                            |
| `PARTIAL`          | Feature is partially implemented or partially verified                         |
| `BLOCKED`          | Feature cannot continue due to missing decision, error, dependency or approval |
| `SETUP_REQUIRED`   | Feature exists or is planned but requires provider/API/config setup            |
| `DEFERRED_TRACKED` | Feature is intentionally deferred but tracked and not skipped                  |
| `DISABLED_BY_FLAG` | Feature is implemented or scaffolded but disabled by feature flag              |
| `NEEDS_REVIEW`     | Feature needs human/admin/legal/security/design review                         |
| `FAILED_QA`        | Feature failed QA and must be fixed                                            |
| `ROLLED_BACK`      | Feature was rolled back                                                        |

---

## 3. QA Status Values

Use only these QA status values:

| QA Status                | Meaning                             |
| ------------------------ | ----------------------------------- |
| `NOT_TESTED`             | QA has not been done                |
| `PASS`                   | QA passed                           |
| `PARTIAL`                | QA partially passed                 |
| `FAIL`                   | QA failed                           |
| `BLOCKED`                | QA could not run                    |
| `NEEDS_MANUAL_CHECK`     | Human/manual verification required  |
| `NEEDS_SECURITY_CHECK`   | Security/RLS verification required  |
| `NEEDS_RESPONSIVE_CHECK` | UI/responsive verification required |
| `NEEDS_PROVIDER_CHECK`   | Real provider verification required |

---

## 4. Global Feature Registry Format

Each feature row must follow this structure:

```md
| ID | Feature | Area | Roles | Routes | DB Objects | Provider | Status | QA | Security/RLS | Notes | Last Updated |
```

Rules:

* Use exact route paths after implementation.
* Use exact table names after implementation.
* Use `TBD` only before implementation.
* Replace `TBD` after implementation.
* Never leave implemented features undocumented.
* Never mark `DONE` without QA status.
* Never mark `PASS` without manual verification or automated test evidence where required.

---

# 38. Final Registry Rule

Before marking any feature as `DONE`, Claude must confirm:

* Code implemented
* DB schema implemented where needed
* SQL migration created where needed
* RLS policy implemented where needed
* Role access enforced server-side
* UI states implemented
* Responsive behavior checked
* No fake UI/data/payment/verification/provider status
* Tests run or documented
* Manual verification updated
* Relevant docs updated
* Pending issues documented

If any requirement is incomplete, mark the feature as:

* `PARTIAL`
* `BLOCKED`
* `SETUP_REQUIRED`
* `DEFERRED_TRACKED`
* or `NEEDS_REVIEW`

Never silently skip or remove it.

## Mandatory Role-Based Home Design Clarification

In addition to all saved docs and prompts, treat role-based home design as mandatory.

Create/design separate role-specific landing/home/dashboard experiences for:

* Guest/Public Home
* Owner Home
* Broker/Agent Home
* Builder/Developer Home

Do not use one generic dashboard/home for all roles.

Each role home must have its own layout, cards, CTAs, modules, quick actions, navigation priorities, real-data/no-data stats, notifications, billing/status blocks, support links, and mobile-first responsive design.

Guest/Public Home must focus on search, city selector, public property/project discovery, login/register popup triggers, SEO sections, public-safe content, and hidden contact protection.

Owner Home must focus on post property, post requirement, own listings, own requirements, leads, inquiries, messages, notifications, billing, profile, verification, and support.

Broker/Agent Home must focus on post property, post requirement, CRM, leads, proposals, messages, site visits, saved searches, billing, verification, public profile, and support.

Builder/Developer Home must focus on post project only, project inventory, project leads, matching buying requirements, proposals, messages, site visits, ads/promotions, RERA/payment status, billing, profile, verification, and support.

All role homes must be mobile-first, responsive, no horizontal scroll, no fake counts, no fake analytics, no fake leads, no fake payment, no fake provider data, and no private/hidden contact leaks.

Implement and verify this requirement during:

* prompts/03_PUBLIC_UI_HOME_HEADER_FOOTER_HERO.md
* prompts/06_OWNER_BROKER_BUILDER_DASHBOARDS.md
* prompts/14_PERFORMANCE_CACHING_DEPLOYMENT_LAUNCH.md
* prompts/15_FINAL_PRODUCTION_API_TESTING_AND_SIGNOFF.md
